Category equalization of ratings with those of the state owner
None of the postal companies currently rated by Standard Poor’s falls into this category
Category notching down with respect to the state owner’s rating
Poste and Poste Italiane currently fall within this category
Category notching up from the postal entity’s standalone rating
The entity’s postal activities are still key public service but the clear aim of the entity is to achieve high level of operational and financial independence either through privatization or commercial autonomy state ownership but independent management

The ratings also take into account the unchallenged status of both it and its parent Germanybased Volkswagen Financial Services AG VWFS as core and captive finance entities to VW the ratings on VW Bank could moderately diverge generally not more than one notch from the ratings on VW or VWFS currently only its outlook differs
The ratings on Germanybased Volkswagen Financial Services AG VWFS are based on its unchallenged status as core subsidiary of German automaker Volkswagen AG VW ANegative and reflect its strategic importance for and close operational integration into its parent

Extracto Ratings direct Poste abril continues to follow topdown rating methodology for Poste which allows for governement supported entity to be rated by up to two categories below the sovereign as we expect the French state to remain Poste’s shareholder in the medium term
The ratings nevertheless already factor in the longterm likelihood of change in the group’s capital structure which would require change in its current établissement public legal status and result in the loss of the state’s ultimate guarantee on LP’s financial obligations the elimination of which was recently recommended by the European Commission
Extracto Ratings direct Poste abril The EC recently recommended that the French government end this guarantee by yearend which they believe provides Poste with more favorable financing conditions than its competitors in market in the process of being liberalized
The ratings on Poste were unaffected by this recommendation since we consider that change in Poste’s status would not necessarily reflect decrease in the strong state support that underpins Poste’s ratings and that has been reaffirmed by recent government decisions
Extracto ADP new enero lowers ratings on Poste with negative outlook The announced legal status and ownership change will give the company greater autonomy from the government which is why its rating has fournotch differential with the rating on the Republic of France rated AAA with stable outlook
P’s negative outlook reflects concerns that the changes in the company’s legal status and ownership likely to take place in the next two years as part of capital hike could pressure the ratings
These initiatives could limit the government’s ability to provide the postal operator with exceptional support without improving its standalone profile in the short term as the capital hike should not decrease Poste’s debt relative to its cash generation

SITUACIÓN MUESTRAS ENSAYO CÁMARA NEBULIZACIÓN
muestras retractores deberán apoyarse suspenderse vertical preferencia paralelas dirección principal flujo horizontal niebla cámara base superficie dominante ensayada

SOLUCIÓN SALINA
solución salina deberá prepararse disolviendo partes cloruro sódico peso partes agua destilada
sal deberá cloruro sódico sustancialmente libre níquel cobre contenido ioduro sódico inferior contenido impurezas seco inferior
solución salina deberá atomizada oC solución resultante pH
AIRE COMPRIMIDO
aire comprimido suministrado inyector inyectores atomizar solución salina deberá libre aceite suciedad mantenido presión kN kN
